<span id="freeTextContainer13265909655069206750">I can’t even this book, it will break your heart and put it back together just in a different way. <br/>I am no stranger to Tymber’s work and this is probably my second favorite book I have ever read/ listened by her. This was the first Audio book by her and I loved it. <br/>You will need tissue this story between Kaden, Seth, and Leah is powerful and heartbreaking. <br/><br/>What would you do if your best friend in the entire world told you he was dying and he need you to fill his shoes so to speak for his wife be</span>
  <span id="freeText13265909655069206750" style="display:none">I can’t even this book, it will break your heart and put it back together just in a different way. <br />I am no stranger to Tymber’s work and this is probably my second favorite book I have ever read/ listened by her. This was the first Audio book by her and I loved it. <br />You will need tissue this story between Kaden, Seth, and Leah is powerful and heartbreaking. <br /><br />What would you do if your best friend in the entire world told you he was dying and he need you to fill his shoes so to speak for his wife because her needs are unique? <br />Not only do you fall in love with Kaden, Leah but you fall in love with Kaden, Seth and Seth, Leah but you also fall in love with the 3 of them as a couple. It’s a beautiful story of love and loss and finding love again. <br />Usually I say quotes I love but I am going to say quotes I loved to hated because they were just too powerful. <br /><br />“Kaden’s dying.”<br />“After”<br />“Hope”<br /><br />Feeling the struggle Seth goes through in this book breaks my heart. I know Leah and Kaden are going through a tough time too. But Seth for me it was more so that he had to come to terms with the end game, and change his life and way of thinking all at the same time. <br /><br />Ok quotes I loved yes I have some! <br /><br />“I’m still not doing you .” - Seth<br />“Still not doing you buddy.” – Kaden<br />“Basic Carpentry in the afternoon, and Sadomasochism 101 in the evening.” - Seth <br /><br />And this one even if it makes me teary<br />“It’s going to rip half my soul out. If you weren't here for me, I would fucking give up and die the minute he quit breathing.” -Leah <br /><br />Also I loved the narration. It was perfect makes you feel apart of the book. I wouldn't chance a thing.<br /><br />P.S. Second Re-read and allllllll the feels.. &lt;3 <br /><br />*You don't have to like my review but its 100% my opinion, and I am allowed to have it.*</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer411607961" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6468255394745188759">There are so many ratings on this that I know I don't have anything new or thought provoking to add...I just want to say that I was surprised how much I truly loved this book. I thought the dynamic between the three main characters was so interesting and beautiful. You could just feel how much they all loved each other, although I think the true love story here was not between Leah and Kaden or Seth, but between Kaden and Seth especially. This was my first Tymber Dalton and I look forward to try</span>
  <span id="freeText6468255394745188759" style="display:none">There are so many ratings on this that I know I don't have anything new or thought provoking to add...I just want to say that I was surprised how much I truly loved this book. I thought the dynamic between the three main characters was so interesting and beautiful. You could just feel how much they all loved each other, although I think the true love story here was not between Leah and Kaden or Seth, but between Kaden and Seth especially. This was my first Tymber Dalton and I look forward to trying another. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('03QZVRYmgCSQRz/UzRv/kNo+YUMh2zylfWl75JTOMdccPV96Z5mfa0rQhKnxUUaujQdtVFo/NY7IAHbeO2qKEg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FHSGQk2SG12uSKcAXFAidmC9Vld6dThBciNoQ33C/OrbPcBtPC0EEnTfHH1gGptIN4RaQAGRMWrHSmV50mZHLw==')})
  }
